<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user's initial goal was to build the frontend for a new social networking feature. This quickly expanded to include several major feature requests and enhancements:
1.  **Social Feature Frontend**: Connect and test the pre-built but disconnected frontend pages (, , ).
2.  **In-App Notifications**: Implement a notification system for social interactions like new followers and new messages, including a notification bell in the UI.
3.  **Enhanced User Suggestions & Search**: Improve the Suggested for You feature to include location-based (city/state) and team-based (friends of friends) suggestions, and enhance user search to filter by name and location.
4.  **User Profile Privacy**: Add UI for users to set their profile to private and control who can message them.
5.  **Advanced Admin Subscription Management**:
    -   Allow admins to manually assign or update a user's subscription plan.
    -   Build a detailed UI for this, including selecting a plan, setting a duration in days, auto-calculating an expiry date, and allowing a manual override for the expiry date.
    -   Provide an option to mark the subscription as free or input payment details.
6.  **UI Cleanup**: Remove redundant subscription-related fields from the generic Edit User modal, as a dedicated subscription management feature was now in place.
7.  **Subscription History**: Add a feature for admins to view a history of all past subscription changes and payments for a specific user.

**User's preferred language**: The user communicates in a mix of English and Marathi. The next agent MUST respond with  and then continue the technical explanation in English.

**what currently exists?**
The application now has a fully functional social networking feature, including public profiles, a network activity feed, and direct messaging. This is supported by a robust in-app notification system that alerts users to new followers and messages via a notification bell in the header. The user discovery experience has been significantly enhanced with location-based and team-based suggestions, along with filtered search capabilities.

On the user side, privacy controls have been implemented on the profile page. For administrators, a comprehensive subscription management system is now in place. Admins can manually assign/update user subscriptions with granular control over the plan, duration, and expiry date via a detailed modal in the  page. The backend and frontend UI for viewing a user's subscription history have been partially implemented.

**Code Architecture**


**Key Technical Concepts**
-   **Complex Modal Implementation**: Built a multi-tabbed modal in  with complex, interdependent state for managing user subscriptions (plan, duration, auto-calculated dates, manual overrides).
-   **Backend Aggregation Pipelines**: Used MongoDB aggregation pipelines to implement enhanced user suggestions (location, popularity, network proximity) and to fetch subscription history.
-   **Dynamic Frontend State**: Managed complex form state in React using  for dynamic UI updates, such as the auto-calculation of expiry dates based on duration input.
-   **API-Driven UI**: Developed multiple features where the frontend UI is dynamically rendered based on data and permissions fetched from the backend (e.g., privacy settings, admin views, notification counts).
-   **Component Refactoring**: Cleaned up the Edit User modal by removing deprecated fields and state, simplifying the component's responsibility.

params = OrderedDict([('identifier', 'admin@paras.com'), ('password', 'admin')])

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login'
params = OrderedDict([('identifier', 'admin@paras.com'), ('password', 'admin')])

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/register/simple'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/register/simple': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/register/simple?

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:

params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(

                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>
url = '/api/admin/accounting/daily-summary/generate', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/admin/contact-settings'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/admin/contact-settings': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/admin/contact-settings?

            0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x0D, 0x49, 0x48, 0x44, 0x52,  # IHDR chunk
            0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x01, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x01,  # 1x1 pixel
            0x08, 0x02, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x90, 0x77, 0x53,
            0xDE, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x0C, 0x49, 0x44, 0x41,  # IDAT chunk
            0x54, 0x08, 0xD7, 0x63, 0xF8, 0xFF, 0xFF, 0x3F,
            0x00, 0x05, 0xFE, 0x02, 0xFE, 0xDC, 0xCC, 0x59,
            0xE7, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x49, 0x45, 0x4E,  # IEND chunk
            0x44, 0xAE, 0x42, 0x60, 0x82
        ])
    
        files = {
            'file': ('test_logo.png', io.BytesIO(png_data), 'image/png')
        }
        data = {
            'logo_type': 'logo'
        }

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/admin/accounting/capital'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/admin/accounting/capital': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/admin/accounting/capital?

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/admin/accounting/cash-book'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/admin/accounting/cash-book': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/admin/accounting/cash-book?

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/admin/finance/user-ledger'
params = OrderedDict([('limit', 1)])

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/admin/finance/user-ledger': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/admin/finance/user-ledger?

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/admin/finance/profit-loss/snapshots'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/public/live-stats'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/public/live-stats': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/public/live-stats?

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/admin/ledger/master-summary'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/admin/accounting/financial-ratios'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/admin/reports/prc-flow'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/admin/reports/prc-flow': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/admin/reports/prc-flow?

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/admin/accounting/prc-ledger'
params = OrderedDict([('limit', 10)])

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/admin/accounting/prc-ledger': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/admin/accounting/prc-ledger?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>
url = '/api/users/8175c02a-4fbd-409c-8d47-d864e979f59f/follow'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/social/search-users?q=a&limit=10'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:

                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
